 der raat sone se pehle ladkiyaan jab 'noti' hoti hai, tab ladke kharrate markar so jate hai
 This mystery is finally solved
 vaigyanikon ne khoj nikaala he ki yah sab hormones kaa khel he jo hamaari 'sex clock' ko bigaadta rahata he
 At about 5 or 6 in the morning, the testosterone levels of boys are at their peak just before they wake up
 is samay purushon main sex hormone din ke baaki ghanton ke mukaable 25 se 50 pratishat adhik banate hai
 Testosterone is also formed in girls for stimulation of sex, but they remain in balance due to estrogen and progesterone
 ladakiyon main iskaa level raat ke samay badhata he
 Research has also shown that the deeper and longer the boys sleep, the more testosterone is produced
 american medical association ki is research ke mutabik 5 ghante se zyada kii neend purushon main testysterone kii maatra ko kareeb 15 fisadi badha sakati he
 The more powerful the sex hormones are in boys, the less in girls when they wake up
 jabaki raat ke samay iskaa ulta hota he
 After 6 o'clock in the evening the testosterone levels in boys begin to fall, while in girls the opposite happens
 unke sex hormones shaam ke baad teji se badhate hai
 The desire for sex in girls increases by 30 percent after the evening turns off by day
 lekin hormones ke level bahari chizon se bhi prabhavit hote hai
 While work tension in the office drops the amount of testosterone in boys, testosterone increases by 20 percent when their favorite sports team wins a match

 Calculate CGPA- Add your grade points to the main five subjects
 iske baad ise paanch se bhaag dijie

 vishay 1: 8, vishay 2:9, vishay 3:7, vishay 4:9, vishay 5:9- pehali step main apane grad paints jodie
 8 + 9 + 7 + 9 + 9 = 42- Divide it by 5 in the second step
 42 / 5 = 8
 5- In this sense your CGPA 8

 When questioned by the opposition's loudness about the reliability of Electronic Voting Machines (evms), the Commission said that it has made public a FAQ list of frequently asked questions to present its views
 haal main ayog ne mashiinon kaa bachaav karte hue do bayaan jari kiye the or mashiinon kii vishwasaneeyata par andeh karne waalon ke jawaab dene ke liye yah teesraa FAQ prayaas he
 Among the questions mentioned in the FAQ, the first question is: can the machine be hacked or not? The Commission's answer is: no
 nirvachan ayog ne bataaya ki iviem kaa em1 model varsh 2006 tak nirmit hua tha or isamen aise sabhi jaruri takanic shaamil kiye gayi the jise kuch logon ke daavon ke vipareet koi hack nahin kar saktaa tha
 The M2 model of EVM was manufactured after the year 2006 and by the year 2012 added additional safety features
 chunaav panel ne kaha, ab isiai-iviem computor sanchalit nahin hai
 These are machines that are neither connected to the Internet nor other networks
 isliye kisi remote upkaran se ise hack kiye jane kii koi sambhaavna nahin he
 
 
 Also, there is no frequency receiver or decoder for wireless or any external hardware port to connect to any other non-evm device or equipment
 baharhaal, ayog ne iviem nirmaataaon dwaara isamen herpher kii ashanka vaale sawaalon ko bhi khaarij kar diya
 The Commission said, this is not possible because evms were manufactured in different years from 2006 and sent to different states
 nirmaataa -bharat electranix limited ,bangalore (biiel) tathaa electronics corporation of india limited, hyderabad (isiaiel) kai saal pehle yah nahin jaan sakati thim ki kisi khaas nirvachan kshetra main koun ummidavaar chunaav ladega or mataptr ikai par ummidavaaron kaa kram kya hoga
 The Commission was asked why developed countries like the US and the European Union did not adopt evms and why some stopped using it

 Appropriate protective measures were not present in their respective laws
 isliye unki adaalaton ne iviem ke istemaal roak diya
